FICHIER: D:\4GI\PO\pick-n-drop\prisma\schema.prisma
================================================================================

// FICHIER: prisma/schema.prisma

generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

// Modèle pour les points relais
model RelayPoint {
  id              Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  name            String
  address         String
  quartier        String
  lat             Float
  lng             Float
  hours           String
  type            RelayPointType
  createdAt       DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime @updatedAt

  departures      Shipment[] @relation("Departures") // Les expéditions qui partent de ce point
  arrivals        Shipment[] @relation("Arrivals")   // Les expéditions qui arrivent à ce point
  staff           User[]                            // Le personnel travaillant dans ce point relais
}

// Modèle pour les utilisateurs / personnel
model User {
  id             Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  email          String   @unique
  name           String
  phone          String?
  passwordHash   String   // Le mot de passe sera haché avant d'être stocké
  role           UserRole
  status         UserStatus @default(OFFLINE)
  avatarUrl      String?
  createdAt      DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime @updatedAt

  relayPoint     RelayPoint? @relation(fields: [relayPointId], references: [id])
  relayPointId   Int?
}

// Modèle central pour une expédition (un colis en transit)
model Shipment {
  id                  Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  trackingNumber      String   @unique
  createdAt           DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt           DateTime @updatedAt

  // Informations sur l'expédition
  status                ShipmentStatus @default(AU_DEPART)
  estimatedArrivalDate  DateTime?
  
  // Détails de l'expéditeur
  senderName        String
  senderPhone       String

  // Détails du destinataire
  recipientName     String
  recipientPhone    String
  
  // Relation avec les points relais
  departurePoint    RelayPoint @relation("Departures", fields: [departurePointId], references: [id])
  departurePointId  Int
  arrivalPoint      RelayPoint @relation("Arrivals", fields: [arrivalPointId], references: [id])
  arrivalPointId    Int

  // Description du colis
  description     String
  weight          Decimal // Utiliser Decimal pour plus de précision que Float
  isFragile       Boolean  @default(false)
  isPerishable    Boolean  @default(false)
  isInsured       Boolean  @default(false)
  declaredValue   Decimal?

  // Informations de paiement
  isPaidAtDeparture Boolean @default(true) // True si payé au départ, false si payé par le destinataire
  shippingCost      Decimal
  amountPaid        Decimal? // Montant réellement perçu
  changeAmount      Decimal? // Monnaie rendue

  // Log de retrait
  withdrawalLog     WithdrawalLog?
}

// Modèle pour enregistrer qui a retiré le colis
model WithdrawalLog {
  id              Int      @id @default(autoincrement())
  retrievalDate   DateTime @default(now())
  
  retirantName    String
  retirantCni     String
  retirantCniDate DateTime
  retirantPhone   String

  shipment        Shipment @relation(fields: [shipmentId], references: [id])
  shipmentId      Int      @unique // Chaque expédition n'a qu'un seul retrait
}


// --- ÉNUMÉRATIONS pour garantir la cohérence des données ---

enum RelayPointType {
  BUREAU
  COMMERCE
  AGENCE
}

enum UserRole {
  MANUTENTIONNAIRE
  RESPONSABLE_STOCK
  SUPERVISEUR
  ACCUEIL_CLIENT
  ADMIN
}

enum UserStatus {
  ONLINE
  PAUSE
  OFFLINE
}

enum ShipmentStatus {
  AU_DEPART
  EN_TRANSIT
  ARRIVE_AU_RELAIS
  RECU
  ANNULE
}

FICHIER: D:\4GI\PO\pick-n-drop\README.md
================================================================================

This is a [Next.js](https://nextjs.org) project bootstrapped with [`create-next-app`](https://nextjs.org/docs/app/api-reference/cli/create-next-app).

## Getting Started

First, run the development server:

```bash
npm run dev
# or
yarn dev
# or
pnpm dev
# or
bun dev
```

Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) with your browser to see the result.

You can start editing the page by modifying `app/page.tsx`. The page auto-updates as you edit the file.

This project uses [`next/font`](https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/optimizing/fonts) to automatically optimize and load [Geist](https://vercel.com/font), a new font family for Vercel.

## Learn More

To learn more about Next.js, take a look at the following resources:

- [Next.js Documentation](https://nextjs.org/docs) - learn about Next.js features and API.
- [Learn Next.js](https://nextjs.org/learn) - an interactive Next.js tutorial.

You can check out [the Next.js GitHub repository](https://github.com/vercel/next.js) - your feedback and contributions are welcome!

## Deploy on Vercel

The easiest way to deploy your Next.js app is to use the [Vercel Platform](https://vercel.com/new?utm_medium=default-template&filter=next.js&utm_source=create-next-app&utm_campaign=create-next-app-readme) from the creators of Next.js.

Check out our [Next.js deployment documentation](https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/deploying) for more details.
